class=\"inner\">\n\t\t<div id=\"news\">\n\t\t\t<h2>News</h2>\n\t\t\t<ul>\n\t\t\t\t<li class=\"n1\"><em>22.3.2017</em><br><h3><a href=\"http://www.smartwings.com/en/news/2017/03/22/smartwings-is-offering-score-of-new-regular-flights-from-france/\">SmartWings is offering a score of new regular flights from France</a></h3><div class=\"news-content\">SmartWings is adding a total of 20 new regular flights from five French airports to its summer schedule. With SmartWings, you can get from Paris directly to Palermo, Brindisi, Heraklion and the Canary Islands – Gran Canaria, Fuerteventura and Lanzarote. From Lille, you will be able to fly with SmartWings to the islands of Mallorca and Tenerife, to Heraklion in Greece and Faro in Portugal. From Lyon, you can get to the Canary Islands – Gran Canaria, Fuerteventura and Tenerife, to Madeira (Funchal) and Palermo. From the airport in Nantes, there will be connections to the Canary Islands – Gran Canaria, Fuerteventura, Tenerife and also to Palermo in Sicily. From Brest, SmartWings is offering a direct flight to Lanzarote.</div></li><li class=\"n2\"><em>10.11.2016</em><br><h3><a href=\"http://www.smartwings.com/en/news/2016/11/10/smartwings-offers-new-direct-flight-from-prague-madrid/\">SmartWings offers new direct flight from Prague to Madrid</a></h3><div class=\"news-content\">SmartWings offers new direct flight from Prague to Madrid. Flight will operate four times per week on monday, thursday, friday and sunday. Tickets can be bought on <a href=\"http://www.smartwings.com\">www.smartwings.com</a> and in travel agencies.</div></li><li class=\"n3\"><em>23.8.2016</em><br><h3><a href=\"http://www.smartwings.com/en/news/2016/08/23/smartwings-offers-tickets-for-summer-2017-season-new-destinations-are-alemria-and-menorca-in-spain-and-lyon-in-france/\">SmartWings offers tickets for a summer 2017 season. New destinations are Almeria and Menorca in Spain and Lyon in France</a></h3><div class=\"news-content\">SmartWings offers tickets to favorite destinations for the summer 2017 season. There are also three new routes available from Prague. First one is to Almeria in Spanish Andalusia, second one is Spanish Menorca and the third one is Lyon in France. Flights to Almeria and Lyon will be available two times per week and to Menorca four times per week. Tickets can be bought on <a href=\"http://www.smartwings.com\">www.smartwings.com</a> or in travel agencies.</div></li><li class=\"n4\"><em>13.6.2016</em><br><h3><a href=\"http://www.smartwings.com/en/news/2016/06/13/smartwings-offers-online-check-in-flights-from-prague/\">SmartWings offers online check-in on flights from Prague</a></h3><div class=\"news-content\">SmartWings starts a new service, <a title=\"online check-in\" href=\"https://checkin.smartwings.com/itraveljs/?lang=en\">online check-in</a>, on Monday June 13th, 2016 on most flights from Prague. This service is available only to passengers on SmartWings regular filghts with a flight numbers in a range QS1000 – 1209 and QS1212 – 1261 and on codeshare flights of partner airlines operated by mentioned SmartWings flights. Passengers can use online check-in from 30 hours prior the scheduled departure and up to 1 hour prior the scheduled departure. It can not be used without a ticket number, for a groups of more than 9 passengers and passengers requiring special services at the airport.</div></li><li class=\"n5\"><em>10.3.2016</em><br><h3><a href=\"http://www.smartwings.com/en/news/2016/03/10/flights-london-twice-day/\">Flights to London twice a day</a></h3><div class=\"news-content\">Thanks to a high demand, SmartWings increases the frequency of flights from Prague to London to twice a day from May 26th, 2016. Tickets can be bought on <a href=\"http://www.smartwings.com\">www.smartwings.com</a> and in travel agencies.</div></li>\t\t\t</ul>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<br><br>\n\t</div>\n</div><!-- #content -->\n\n<div id=\"sidebar\">\n\t<div class=\"inner\">\n\n\t\t<br>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div id=\"newsletter\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<form method=\"post\" action=\"http://newsletter.smartwings.com/web_subscribe.php\" class=\"form form-newsletter\" id=\"form_newsletter\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<fieldset>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h3>Newsletter</h3>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<input type=\"email\" name=\"email\" id=\"email_newsletter\" value=\"\" placeholder=\"email@example.com\"><br>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<button type=\"submit\" name=\"send_form\">subscribe</button>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<input type=\"hidden\" name=\"language\" id=\"language_newsletter\" value=\"en\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<input type=\"hidden\" name=\"send_from\" value=\"newsletter\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</fieldset>\n\t\t\t\t\t</form>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\t\t<br>\n\n\t\t<a class=\"seatnfood\" href=\"http://bookings.smartwings.com/en/checkmytripin.php\">\n\t\t\t<p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<img src=\"http://www.smartwings.com/ipp/content/themes/smartwings/images/sw-seat-food-en.png\" alt=\"Select a seat.
